### [151] [Aziz and Howl's Gravity-Induced Entanglement Channel is Essentially Classical Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16276)
*Hanyu Xue,Ziqian Tang,Chen Yang,Zizhao Han,Zikuan Kan,Yulong Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 对Aziz和Howl关于引力场产生量子纠缠的论文进行批判性分析，指出其理论解释错误且计算存在放大效应的问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Aziz和Howl声称经典引力场可以通过量子场论通道产生量子纠缠，但本文作者认为需要重新审视这一结论的正确性

Method: 通过理论分析指出原论文的缺陷：1）将半经典波包运动误认为量子场论效应；2）使用不连续波函数导致计算放大；3）提出使用高斯波包进行正确计算

Result: 原论文的量子纠缠效应被错误放大，正确使用高斯波包计算后，引力场产生的量子纠缠效应将变得微乎其微

Conclusion: Aziz和Howl的结论存在根本性错误，经典引力场实际上无法产生显著的量子纠缠效应

Abstract: Aziz and Howl argued that a classical gravitational field can generate quantum entanglement through a quantum-field-theoretic channel mediated by virtual matter propagation. However, their claimed channel is more naturally and accurately understood as semiclassical wavepacket motion in an external gravitational field, rather than as a distinctively quantum-field-theoretic entangling effect. Moreover, the result of their perturbative computation is incorrectly magnified: they selected a discontinuous wavefunction with infinite kinetic energy as the initial state and simultaneously treated it as stationary. Once a correct treatment using Gaussian wavepacket is adapted, the resulting effect will be negligibly small.

</details>


### [152] [Boson correlations are spurious for classical states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16283)
*Daniel E. Salazar,Fabrice P. Laussy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 玻色子相关性是辛普森悖论的体现：它们是从不同几何构型中无关联测量的统计平均产生的虚假相关性，对称性破缺是混杂因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示玻色子相关性的本质，区分量子平均与统计平均，为理解非经典性和量子优势提供新视角。

Method: 分析具有Glauber-Sudarshan表示的量子态密度矩阵，包括相干态、热态等经典态，证明其相关性是统计平均的产物。

Result: 玻色子相关性是辛普森悖论的体现：波函数编码的相关性出现在假定的几何构型中，但该几何构型并非统计系综的几何，而是随实现而变化。

Conclusion: 需要区分量子平均和统计平均，这为理解非经典性和量子优势提供了新的基础性认识。

Abstract: We show that boson correlations from quantum states with a Glauber-Sudarshan representation of their density matrix which provides a well-behaved probability distribution -- including coherent states, thermal states, and all states that can be deemed classical -- are a manifestation of the Simpson paradox: they are spurious correlations from statistical (ensemble) averages over uncorrelated measurements made in varying geometries, due to a process of symmetry-breaking as a confounding factor. Bosonic correlations encoded by the wavefunction appear to be formed in the geometry assumed, which however is not that of the statistical ensemble but varies from realization to realization. This calls to distinguish between quantum and statistical averages and sheds new understandings on the fundamental problems of nonclassicality and quantum advantage.

</details>


### [153] [How to unitarily map between any two pure states with a single closed-form exponential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16285)
*Peter T. J. Bradshaw,Marcus Gouveia,Jonte R. Hance*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种基于代数方法的封闭形式指数酉变换，无需显式基即可将任意两个纯量子态相互映射，且复杂度与希尔伯特空间维度无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法需要为初始态和目标态分别提供显式基，复杂度随希尔伯特空间维度增长。需要一种更高效、与维度无关的方法来构造纯态之间的酉变换。

Method: 利用新颖的代数方法构造封闭形式的指数酉变换，仅使用单个酉生成元，不依赖于任何基的选择，且与希尔伯特空间维度无关。

Result: 成功构建了通用的封闭形式指数酉变换，能够将任意两个纯量子态相互映射，且构造过程独立于基的选择和希尔伯特空间维度。

Conclusion: 该方法为量子信息论中研究纯态系统关系提供了有用工具，同时可用于量子电路和酉算子的基本分析，具有广泛的应用价值。

Abstract: It is well-known that any two pure quantum states (in the same Hilbert space) can be mapped to any other using unitary transformations. However, previous approaches to this problem required two explicit bases for the Hilbert space, one each for the initial and target states, and thus their complexity necessarily scales with the dimension of the Hilbert space. In this Letter, we show how to utilize novel algebraic methods to construct a closed-form exponential unitary transformation which achieves this in general, using only a single unitary generator. This construction is independent of any bases and agnostic to the dimension of the Hilbert space. We highlight the usefulness of this tool for studying relationships between systems of pure states in quantum information theory, as well in elementary analyses of quantum circuits and unitary operators.

</details>


### [154] [Fast, High-Fidelity Erasure Detection of Dual-Rail Qubits with Symmetrically Coupled Readout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16292)
*Jimmy Shih-Chun Hung,Arbel Haim,Mouktik Raha,Gihwan Kim,Ziwen Huang,Ming-Han Chou,Mitch D'Ewart,Erik Davis,Anurag Mishra,Patricio Arrangoiz Arriola,Amirhossein Khalajhedayati,David Hover,Fernando G. S. L. Brandão,Aashish A. Clerk,Alex Retzker,Harry Levine,Oskar Painter*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文实现了基于双轨量子比特的擦除检测，通过对称耦合的读出谐振器实现了快速、高保真度的单次擦除检测，并展示了与单量子比特门并行的时间连续擦除检测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 擦除量子比特是实现硬件高效量子纠错的有前景平台，但要发挥其纠错优势需要快速、高保真度且可扩展的中电路擦除检查。

Method: 采用硬件高效的电路设计：单个读出谐振器与双轨量子比特的两个transmon进行色散对称耦合，实现单次擦除检测和时间连续擦除检测。

Result: 实现了384纳秒的单次擦除检测，每次检查的残余误差为6.0(2)×10⁻⁴，诱导退相干仅为8(3)×10⁻⁵，擦除误差为2.54(1)×10⁻²。时间连续检测中，单量子比特门的中位误差为7.2×10⁻⁵，擦除检测诱导误差小于1×10⁻⁵。

Conclusion: 对称耦合色散读出是快速、硬件高效且可扩展的组件，为基于transmon双轨量子比特的擦除量子纠错提供了关键要素。

Abstract: Erasure qubits are a promising platform for implementing hardware-efficient quantum error correction. Realizing the error-correction advantages of this encoding requires frequent mid-circuit erasure checks that are fast, high-fidelity, and scalable. Here, we realize erasure detection with a hardware-efficient circuit consisting of a single readout resonator dispersively and symmetrically coupled to both transmons of a dual-rail qubit. We use this circuit to demonstrate single-shot erasure detection in 384 ns with minimal impact on the dual-rail logical manifold, achieving a residual error per check of $6.0(2) \times 10^{-4}$, with only $8(3) \times 10^{-5}$ induced dephasing per check, and an erasure error per check of $2.54(1)\times 10^{-2}$. The high degree of matched dispersive readout coupling ($χ$-matching) within the dual-rail qubit code space also allows us to realize a new modality: time-continuous erasure detection performed in parallel with single-qubit gates. Here we achieve a median $7.2 \times 10^{-5}$ error per gate with $< 1 \times 10^{-5}$ error induced by erasure detection. This demonstrates a reduction in erasure detection overhead as well as a crucial ingredient for soft information quantum error correction. Together, these results establish symmetrically coupled dispersive readout as a fast, hardware-efficient, and scalable component for erasure-based quantum error correction using transmon dual-rail qubits.

</details>
